### [168] [X+Slides: Benchmarking Audience-Conditioned Slide Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19256)
*Haodong Chen,Xuanhe Zhou,Wei Zhou,Xinyue Shao,Yanbing Zhu,Bo Wang,Jiawei Hong,Anya Jia,Fan Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出X+Slides基准，用于评估面向受众的幻灯片自动生成，通过动态评估框架和四个互补指标弥补现有基准忽视目标受众的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准只评估幻灯片的完整性和技术深度，忽视了目标受众这一关键因素（如专家需要严格证明，决策者需要可操作结论），缺乏面向受众的评估方法。

Method: 构建X+Slides基准，包含113个主题和7种展示场景的多样化语料库，利用8,133个去重且基于源文的探针，通过为同一探针分配不同受众的效用权重，实现受众条件化的动态评估，并提出四个指标：受众覆盖率、领域覆盖率、效率、正确性。

Result: 在DeepPresenter、SlideTailor和NotebookLM上的实验表明，当前系统能恢复大部分但非全部受众关键信息：在τ_A=0.7阈值下，DeepPresenter最好受众覆盖率为0.714，SlideTailor为0.594，NotebookLM消融版本达0.853但存在明显的接地差异。

Conclusion: 视觉质量和广泛主题覆盖不应被视为源文支持的证据，必须结合基于源文的评估来验证幻灯片声称的正确性。

Abstract: Automatically generating slide decks from source documents is an important application of large language models (LLMs). Existing benchmarks primarily assess slide completeness and technical depth, while overlooking the target audience as a critical real-world factor. For instance, specialists demand rigorous proofs, whereas decision-makers prioritize actionable conclusions. To bridge this gap, we introduce X+Slides, a benchmark specifically designed for audience-conditioned slide generation. Built on a diverse corpus spanning 113 topics and seven presentation scenes, X+Slides employs a dynamic evaluation framework constructed from 8,133 deduplicated, source-grounded probes. By assigning audience-specific utility weights to the same source-grounded probes, X+Slides reports four complementary metrics: Audience Coverage measures how much audience-essential information is conveyed, Domain-wise Coverage shows which information types are covered, Efficiency measures delivered utility per unit of attention cost, and Correctness verifies whether slide claims are supported by the source. Experiments on DeepPresenter, SlideTailor, and NotebookLM show that current systems can recover a substantial but still incomplete part of audience-essential information: at $τ_A=0.7$, DeepPresenter reaches a best Audience Coverage of 0.714, SlideTailor reaches 0.594, and the NotebookLM ablation reaches 0.853 while showing clear grounding differences. These results indicate that visual quality and broad topic coverage should not be treated as evidence support without source-grounded evaluation.

### [169] [NeSyCat Torch: A Differentiable Tensor Implementation of Categorical Semantics for Neurosymbolic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19279)
*Daniel Romero Schellhorn,Till Mossakowski,Björn Gehrke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NeSyCat Torch 通过单子（monad）参数化，将神经符号语义统一在单一归纳定义下，支持模糊、概率、经典和神经系统的真值定义，并通过惰性对数张量单子和批处理单子实现可微分训练，在 MNIST 加法任务上优于 LTN 和 DeepProbLog，接近 DeepStochLog 精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经符号语义碎片化，不同系统（经典、模糊、概率、神经）各自定义真值，缺乏统一框架；且 NeSyCat 此前缺少对神经网络学习谓词和函数的支持。

Method: 提出 NeSyCat Torch，通过强单子（strong monad）和真值上的聚合结构参数化，统一各类语义；使用分布单子作为参考语义和度量评估，引入惰性对数张量单子（lazy log-tensor monad over log-semiring）实现数值稳定和可微分训练，并通过批处理单子（batch monad）实现高效批量训练。公理即源代码，以单子 do-notation 编写，单子绑定自动执行边缘化和惰性剪枝。

Result: 在 MNIST 加法任务上，HaskTorch、JAX 和 PyTorch 实现在速度和准确率上均优于 LTN 和 DeepProbLog，准确率接近 DeepStochLog。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一个统一的、参数化于单子的神经符号框架，可适用于多种一阶 NeSy 方法；未来工作可扩展至连续概率（如 Giry 单子）的神经表示。

Abstract: Neurosymbolic semantics is fragmented: classical, fuzzy, probabilistic and neural systems each define truth by their own inductive rules. NeSyCat, extending ULLER, subsumes them under a single inductive definition of truth, parametric in a strong monad and an aggregation structure on truth-values. NeSyCat has so far lacked an account of predicates and functions learned by neural networks.
  We provide NeSyCat Torch as the missing link and interpret computational symbols via neural networks, implementing the framework in probabilistic programming and tensor-based backends. We use the distribution monad for reference semantics and metric evaluation, and complement it by a monad for numerically stable, differentiable training: the lazy log-tensor monad over the log-semiring. For efficient training in batches, we furthermore employ a batch monad. The axioms are the source code: written once in monad-based do-notation, monadic bind performs marginalisation, lazily pruning unneeded branches.
  On MNIST addition, our HaskTorch, JAX, and PyTorch implementations outperform LTN and DeepProbLog in speed and accuracy, while achieving nearly the accuracy of DeepStochLog. However, unlike DeepStochLog, we stay in a uniform framework that applies to many first-order NeSy approaches. Namely, the construction is parametric in the monad; instantiating it with, e.g., the Giry monad extends the approach to continuous probability (working out a neural representation here is left for future work).

</details>


### [170] [Rethinking Reward Supervision: Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19327)
*Siyi Gu,Jialin Chen,Sophia Zhou,Arman Cohan,Rex Ying*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation框架，通过结构化评分准则(rubrics)提供细粒度反馈，替代传统标量奖励或单一推理链蒸馏，在科学推理基准上平均超越GRPO 1.0个点、OPSD 0.9个点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理语言模型的后训练方法存在两大问题：(1)监督蒸馏依赖昂贵且可能含噪声的思维链标注；(2)基于验证奖励的强化学习将评估反馈压缩为标量信号，掩盖了响应中具体需要改进的方面。

Method: 提出Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation框架：(1)两阶段流程——先学习生成任务特定的rubrics，再训练rubric引导的推理器；(2)教师模型基于rubrics为学生的采样轨迹提供token级指导；(3)避免将单一参考推理链作为唯一监督目标，利用rubrics定义优质响应应满足的标准，实现比标量奖励优化更细粒度的信用分配。

Result: 在多个科学推理基准上，rubric条件自蒸馏方法平均超越GRPO 1.0个点，超越OPSD 0.9个点。

Conclusion: Rubric-conditioned self-distillation能有效将rubric级标准转化为推理过程中的token级指导，验证了结构化细粒度反馈相比标量奖励和单一蒸馏目标的优越性。

Abstract: Post-training of reasoning language models is commonly driven by supervised distillation and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. Distillation often relies on chain-of-thought annotations that are expensive to obtain and may themselves be noisy, incomplete, or partially incorrect; even when the final solution is correct, an imperfect rationale can interfere with learning. Reinforcement learning with verified rewards, on the other hand, typically compresses evaluative feedback into a scalar signal, obscuring which aspects of a response should be improved. We propose \textbf{Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation}, a framework that incorporates rubrics as structured, fine-grained feedback for on-policy self-distillation. Our method conditions the teacher model on criterion-level rubrics and uses it to provide token-level guidance on the student's own sampled trajectories. This design avoids treating a single reference rationale as the sole supervision target. Instead, rubrics specify what a strong response should satisfy, enabling more fine-grained credit assignment over the reasoning process than scalar reward optimization. We instantiate this framework with a two-stage pipeline that first learns to generate task-specific rubrics and then trains a rubric-guided reasoner. We evaluate on a diverse suite of science reasoning benchmarks and results show that rubric-conditioned self-distillation effectively converts rubric-level criteria into token-level guidance over the reasoning process, surpassing GRPO by 1.0 points and OPSD by 0.9 points on average.

</details>

### [171] [Mitigating Anchoring Bias in LLM-Based Agents for Energy-Efficient 6G Autonomous Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18272)
*Hatim Chergui,Claudia Carballo González,Farhad Rezazadeh,Merouane Debbah*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于LLM代理的自主资源协商框架，用于6G网络零接触切片。针对LLM代理的锚定偏差导致网络过度配置问题，作者提出了一种截断三参数威布尔分布的随机锚定策略，并结合CVaR数字孪生保障SLA尾延迟。证明了双峰约束避免效用定理，实验表明该方法打破刚性协商模式，节省高达25%能耗，且1B参数模型推理延迟低于1秒，适用于O-RAN非实时RIC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 6G架构需要零接触网络切片，但现有LLM代理在资源协商中存在锚定偏差（anchoring bias），即僵化地坚持初始启发式方案，导致严重的网络过度配置（over-provisioning），造成资源浪费。作者希望系统性地缓解这一认知偏差，实现高效、节能的网络切片协商。

Method: 1) 提出随机锚定策略，使用截断三参数威布尔分布（Truncated 3-Parameter Weibull distribution）建模，数学上有界地缓解锚定偏差。2) 结合基于条件风险价值（CVaR）的突发感知数字孪生（Burst-aware DTs），严格保障SLA尾延迟。3) 提出并证明双峰约束避免效用定理（Bimodal Constraint-Avoidance Utility Theorem），揭示可行协商遵循凸边界，高约束场景经历相变并服从逆有理衰减包络。4) 使用本地部署的1B参数模型（otel-llm-1b-it）进行实验验证。

Result: 认知去偏策略成功瓦解了代理的刚性协商模式，迫使代理主动探索并安全地接近SLA边界，系统能耗节省高达25%。轻量级1B LLM推理延迟平均仅0.95秒，满足O-RAN非实时RIC的操作时标要求。

Conclusion: 提出的去偏随机锚定框架能有效克服LLM代理在6G网络切片中的锚定偏差，在保障SLA的同时显著提升能效。轻量级模型保证了实时可行性，为6G零接触网络切片提供了有前景的方案。

Abstract: This paper presents an autonomous agentic resource negotiation framework designed to enable zero-touch network slicing in 6G architectures using Large Language Model (LLM) agents. While LLMs offer powerful reasoning capabilities, we demonstrate that such agents inherently suffer from anchoring bias, rigidly adhering to initial heuristic proposals and causing severe network over-provisioning. To systematically mitigate this cognitive bias, we propose a novel randomized anchoring strategy modeled via a Truncated 3-Parameter Weibull distribution. This mathematically bounded approach seamlessly integrates with burst-aware Digital Twins (DTs) employing Conditional Value at Risk (CVaR) to rigorously guarantee strict Service Level Agreement (SLA) tail-latencies. To validate our methodology, we introduce and prove the \emph{Bimodal Constraint-Avoidance Utility Theorem}, demonstrating that while feasible negotiations follow classical convex bounds, highly constrained scenarios undergo a phase transition governed by an inverse rational decay envelope. Empirical results generated using a locally hosted 1B-parameter model (\texttt{otel-llm-1b-it}) confirm these dual-regime bounds. Our cognitive de-biasing successfully dismantles rigid negotiation patterns, forcing agents into active exploration to safely ride SLA boundaries and boost system energy savings up to 25\%. Crucially, the lightweight 1B LLM achieves sub-second inference latencies (0.95s mean), ensuring our multi-agent framework is compatible with the operational timescales of the O-RAN non-Real-Time RAN Intelligent Controller (non-RT RIC)\footnote{Our source code is available for non-commercial use at https://github.com/HatimChergui.

### [172] [Robustness Analysis of Australia's Internet Using a Multilayer Network Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18737)
*Benjamin Lang,Matthew Roughan,Mengbin Ye*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文构建了澳大利亚六大ISP的多层网络模型，分析表明网络多样性提供了冗余性，即使在共享风险链路组（SRLG）故障下也是如此，强调了多样化网络生态系统的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究澳大利亚互联网基础设施中独立提供商网络之间的互联关系，特别是探究对等互联如何提供单网故障冗余，以及共享风险链路组（SRLG）可能引入的潜在脆弱性。

Method: 提出一个广义多层网络模型，每层代表一个ISP网络，并包含一个IXP层用于互联。构建了包含六大主要ISP的澳大利亚特定模型，并进行故障分析。

Result: 故障分析表明，即使存在共享风险，网络多样性仍能提供冗余性，证明了多样化网络生态系统的重要性。

Conclusion: 多样化网络生态对提升基础设施韧性至关重要，即使面对共享物理依赖（如共用管道）引发的SRLG故障，网络多样性也能有效增强冗余。

Abstract: Australia depends on an Internet built from multiple networks of long-haul links. We study the interactions of these independent provider networks to investigate how the peering between these networks provides redundancy for failures on a single network, as well as the potential vulnerabilities introduced by failures of Shared Risk Link Groups (SRLGs), whereby ostensibly independent links of different providers fail simultaneously due to joint physical dependencies such as shared conduits. We introduce a generalised multilayer network model in which each layer represents the network of an individual Internet Service Provider (ISP), along with an Internet Exchange Point (IXP) layer that facilitates interconnections between ISP networks. We construct an Australia-specific model, consisting of six major ISPs. A failure analysis is performed on this network, revealing that diversity provides redundancy, even in the presence of shared risks, indicating the importance of a diverse network ecosystem.

### [177] [Simulating Hate Speech Cascades with Multi-LLM Agents: Empirical Grounding, Modeling Fidelity, and Intervention Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18264)
*Fan Huang*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究多智能体LLM系统能否比经典级联模型更忠实地模拟仇恨内容传播。通过Bluesky数据发现仇恨级联具有立场单一、毒性同质性高、星型拓扑等特征，多LLM智能体模拟器成功复现了立场单一性和毒性差异方向。消融实验表明智能体异质性是关键因素，针对性放大器策略在密集网络上可实现7.5-12.9%的传播减少，附带5.7%良性误伤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有级联模型未明确表征用户画像、社区和内容因素，导致其在真实场景中策略效果不佳。探索多智能体LLM系统是否能更忠实地模拟仇恨内容传播。

Method: 对比分析Bluesky上3个仇恨级联与1个良性级联的实证数据，构建多LLM智能体模拟器进行仿真，并通过结构化消融实验分析影响保真度的关键因素。

Result: 实证发现：97.4-99.7%转发者持敌对立场；仇恨级联中毒性-参与同质性在传播树上高于关注图；仇恨级联呈星型拓扑，良性级联呈树型拓扑。模拟器成功复现了立场单一性和毒性差异方向。消融实验识别出智能体异质性为关键保真度因素。

Conclusion: 多智能体LLM系统能比经典模型更忠实地模拟仇恨内容传播，其中智能体异质性至关重要。基于此的放大器策略在密集网络上可有效减少传播。

Abstract: Faithful modeling of hateful content propagation on online platforms remains an open problem for moderation research. Classical cascade models that do not explicitly represent the profile, community, and content factors associated with hateful-content propagation may yield moderation strategies that behave less effectively when deployed in real-world scenarios. Multi-agent large language model (LLM) systems can, in principle, make each reshare decision depend on the user's profile, the surrounding community, and the post's content, but it remains unclear whether this added flexibility actually reproduces real hateful cascades more faithfully than classical baselines. We study three hateful Bluesky cascades and a size-matched benign control. In the empirical Bluesky data, we found that: 97.4--99.7\% of reposters take a hostile stance; toxicity-engagement homophily is higher on the diffusion tree than on the follower graph for hateful cascades; topology is star-like for the hateful cascades (most reposts come directly from the root) versus tree-like for the benign cascade (reposts propagate through multi-hop chains). In simulation, a multi-LLM-agent simulator reproduces the stance monoculture and the toxicity-delta direction. A structured ablation identifies agent heterogeneity as the leading fidelity factor, and amplifier targeting on dense networks yields 7.5--12.9\% reduction at 5.7\% benign collateral.

### [178] [Graph Instance Landscapes: When Structural Similarity Does (Not) Reflect Shortest-Path Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18267)
*Maryam Gholami Shiri,Ivana Krminac,Marko Djukanović,Sašo Džeroski,Eva Tuba,Tome Eftimov*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文采用实例景观视角，通过低代价结构特征空间嵌入图并聚类成结构相似区域，对四种最短路径算法在三种图集上的性能进行结构化基准测试分析，发现特征空间相似性并不必然意味着性能相似性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统最短路径算法基准测试基于异构图集的整体性能聚合，无法揭示不同搜索范式如何响应实例结构特征，因此需要一种结构感知的基准测试方法。

Method: 将图嵌入低代价的结构特征空间，聚类为结构相似区域；在加权Erdős–Rényi图、随机几何图（无线图）和真实道路网络三种图集上，评估Dijkstra、双向Dijkstra、A*和DEQ四种求解器；通过多种特征选择方案分析聚类鲁棒性，并使用非参数检验比较不同景观区域的运行时分布。

Result: 生成器参数能诱导稳定的结构区域，但特征空间相似性并不必然意味着性能相似性；即使在相同的景观区域内，也经常观察到显著的运行时变化；不同基准图族在特征空间中占据大部分不相交的区域。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了结构景观在最短路径算法结构化基准测试中的潜力和局限性。

Abstract: Benchmarking shortest-path algorithms is commonly based on aggregate performance over heterogeneous graph sets, which limits insight into how different search paradigms react to instance structure. We adopt an instance-landscape view of graph benchmarking by embedding graphs into a low-cost structural feature space and clustering them into regions of similar structure. Three benchmark suites are studied: weighted Erdős--Rényi graphs, random geometric (wireless) graphs, and real-world road networks. We evaluate four representative shortest-path solvers spanning uninformed exact search (Dijkstra), bidirectional exact search (bidirectional Dijkstra), heuristic-guided exact search (A$^{*}$), and deque-based strategies (DEQ). Clustering robustness is analyzed under multiple feature-selection schemes, and runtime distributions are compared across landscape regions using non-parametric tests. While generator parameters induce stable structural regions, we find that feature-space similarity does not necessarily imply performance similarity: significant runtime shifts are frequently observed even within the same landscape region. A merged-suite analysis further shows that different benchmark families occupy largely disjoint regions. These results highlight both the potential and the limits of structural landscapes for the structure-aware benchmarking of shortest-path algorithms.

### [180] [HyDRA: Lossless Hypergraph Summarization via Co-Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18274)
*Giulia Preti,Aris Anagnostopoulos,Francesco Bonchi*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: HyDRA是首个用于加权超图的无损摘要框架，通过超节点和超超边分组结合修正表实现精确重构，采用参数自由的贪心算法高效压缩，可降低80-93%的存储成本，并支持直接查询与下游任务加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超图能有效表示高阶交互关系，但其规模和复杂性带来了数据管理和分析的挑战。虽然图摘要技术已被广泛用于简化简单图，但超图的无损摘要问题尚未被探索。

Method: 建立了超图摘要与共聚类的概念联系，设计了一种参数自由的贪心算法，通过迭代合并节点簇和超边簇来最小化一种新的存储感知成本函数，并采用增量更新策略避免每次迭代重新计算修正表。

Result: 实验表明HyDRA在不同超图特征下可减少80-93%的存储成本；生成的摘要本身是超图，可直接查询，为各种连通性和中心性查询提供快速准确的近似答案，并加速影响最大化等下游任务。

Conclusion: HyDRA是首个加权超图无损摘要框架，兼具高压缩率与实用性，为超图的高效存储、查询和分析提供了一种有效解决方案。

Abstract: Hypergraphs are a powerful representation for higher-order interactions but their scale and complexity pose significant data management and analysis challenges. While summarization techniques are widely used to distill simple graphs, lossless summarization for hypergraphs remains unexplored. We introduce HyDRA, the first formal framework for lossless summarization of weighted hypergraphs. In our framework, a summary is a new weighted hypergraph composed of supernodes (groups of nodes) and superhyperedges (groups of hyperedges), paired with a correction table for exact reconstruction. By establishing a conceptual link to co-clustering, we design an efficient, parameter-free greedy algorithm that iteratively merges node and hyperedge clusters to minimize a novel storage-aware cost function. HyDRA employs an incremental update strategy to prevent the costly recomputation of the correction table at each step. Extensive experiments demonstrate that \our achieves a substantial reduction in storage cost (80-93% in some settings, depending on the hypergraph characteristics). Because the resulting summaries are themselves hypergraphs, they can be queried directly, providing fast and accurate approximate answers for various connectivity and centrality queries, and accelerating downstream tasks such as influence maximization.

### [181] [Joint Discovery of Graph Structure and Dynamics in Stochastic Interacting Particle Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18279)
*Demao Liu,Ting Gao,Jinqiao Duan*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机相互作用粒子系统中网络结构与演化动力学的联合识别问题，提出了两种交替最小二乘估计器（TALS和IALS），并建立了在秩-2联合强制条件下的可辨识性理论，通过合成实验和真实SEEG数据验证了方法的有效性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常将图结构推断与动力学参数估计分开处理，缺乏对二者耦合关系的理论保障，且难以同时处理局部与非局部相互作用成分。

Method: 将问题建模为图与基系数的耦合逆问题，提出三块交替最小二乘（TALS）和集成对角增强最小二乘（IALS）两种估计器，后者将局部和相互作用系数更新融合为单一子问题，并建立了基于秩-2联合强制条件的可辨识性理论。

Result: 合成实验表明两种估计器能准确恢复交互图和动力学成分，且对随机强迫、观测噪声和基失配具有鲁棒性；真实SEEG数据应用展示了稳定且可解释的动力学摘要。

Conclusion: 该工作为随机相互作用粒子系统的学习提供了有理论保证的可扩展框架，在计算生物学、神经科学等领域具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: We study the joint identification of network structure and governing dynamics in stochastic interacting particle systems, which consist of an unknown directed weighted interaction graph with unknown local and non-local interaction components. We formulate the problem as a coupled inverse problem for the graph and the associated basis coefficients, and develop two alternating least-squares-type estimators: a three-block scheme (TALS) and an integrated diagonal-augmented scheme (IALS). The IALS formulation combines the updates of the local and interaction coefficients into a single least-squares subproblem, and is particularly well suited to settings in which the nodewise local dynamics share a common functional template up to node-dependent scaling. We further establish an identifiability result under a rank-2 joint coercivity condition together with an appropriate normalization convention. Synthetic experiments show that the proposed estimators accurately recover both the interaction graph and the dynamical components, and remain robust under stochastic forcing, observation noise, and basis mismatch. We also provide an illustrative real-data application on ictal SEEG recordings, where the learned models produce stable and interpretable dynamical summaries across multiple basis configurations. This work advances a theoretically guaranteed scalable framework for learning stochastic interacting particle systems, with broad potential for data-driven identification in computational biology, neuroscience, and beyond.

</details>


### [182] [A Stochastic ISCS Markov Model for Fake News Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18282)
*Carles Rovira*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文基于马尔可夫链和扩展的Daley-Kendall模型（ISCS框架），研究了事实核查者对虚假新闻传播动力学的影响，并通过数值模拟验证了相关结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚假新闻的传播对社会造成严重危害，而经典模型缺乏对事实核查机制的系统性建模，因此需要在随机传播模型中引入核查者角色，以更真实地刻画谣言抑制过程。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链构建随机谣言传播模型，基于Piqueira (2020)的ISCS（Ignorant/Spreader/Checker/Stifler）框架，对Daley-Kendall模型进行推广，并通过数值模拟分析系统行为。

Result: 数值模拟展示了事实核查者对虚假新闻传播动态的影响，验证了模型的有效性。

Conclusion: 事实核查者能有效抑制虚假新闻的传播，该随机模型为理解谣言动力学提供了理论工具。

Abstract: This paper studies the propagation of fake news through a stochastic rumor spreading model based on Markov chains. Inspired by classical epidemiological SIR models, we consider a generalization of the Daley-Kendall framework for rumours that incorporates fact-checkers, following the Ignorant/Spreader/Checker/Stifler model introduced in Piqueira (2020). The model analyzes the influence of checkers on fake news dynamics. Numerical simulations are used to illustrate the behavior of the system and the impact of fact-checkers.

</details>


### [183] [RELIANCE: Curating and Evaluating Reproductive Health Information on Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18285)
*Vaibhav Balloli,Laura Peyton Ellis,Vishala Mishra,Alice Chi,Alex Peahl,Elizabeth Bondi-Kelly*

Main category: cs.SI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体（如TikTok）已成为健康信息的重要来源，但存在信息不准确问题。LLM被集成到数字平台进行事实核查，但在生殖健康等关键领域缺乏严格评估可能造成严重危害。因此需要构建专业标注数据集来评估LLM的事实核查能力。

Method: 构建了一个专家标注的数据集，包含409个标注句子，来自336个视频和56个经临床医生审核的查询。由三名妇产科及内科专家进行标注。数据集用于分析生殖健康信息现状并评估LLM的事实核查能力。

Conclusion: 该数据集和方法能支持机器学习社区改进LLM在重要领域的应用，可扩展到其他平台和语言，并帮助健康社区进一步理解社交媒体上的信息环境。

Abstract: Social media platforms like TikTok have become a key source of health information, with studies reporting inaccuracies in posts. As Large Language Model (LLM) providers increasingly integrate LLMs into digital platforms to fact-check content (e.g., Grok and Perplexity on X and WhatsApp, respectively) and are being used by people to fact-check information, deploying these systems in critical areas such as reproductive health without rigorous evaluation can cause serious harm. We introduce RELIANCE, an expert-annotated dataset of health information on TikTok surrounding pregnancy and postpartum queries, serving as both an analysis of the reproductive health information landscape and an evaluation of LLMs' capabilities in fact-checking this content. Our dataset comprises 409 annotated sentences from 336 videos across 56 clinician-reviewed queries, annotated by three expert clinicians in Obstetrics, Gynecology, and Internal Medicine. Our findings reveal that nearly 60\% of the health information in the videos we sampled is accurate. Furthermore, LLM evaluations reveal a gap between evaluating specific claims and evaluating the entire content (15\%). We believe that our methodology, dataset, and tool will support the machine learning community in improving LLMs for important domains with real-world data, extending to other platforms and languages, and helping the health community further understand the information landscape on social media. Our dataset and code are made available at https://realize-lab.github.io/RELIANCE/.

### [184] [Co-evolution of the global research collaboration network and the performance of nations in science and technology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18549)
*Travis A. Whetsell,Jeongyoon,Yang*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本研究使用纵向共演化模型分析了1993-2022年166个国家的数据，证实了国际研究合作网络与国家科研绩效之间存在双向因果关系的共演化现象，并发现地理距离会调节这种互动关系，使研究者更依赖可见的绩效指标来选择远距离合作者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来研究者怀疑国际合作与科研绩效之间存在双向因果关系，但缺乏大规模实证验证。本研究旨在通过纵向数据同时检验这两种现象的共演化过程。

Method: 采用随机行动者导向模型（SAOM），分析1993-2022年166个国家的纵向数据。国际合作网络来自Web of Science的XML数据库，科研绩效数据来自Elsevier的分领域加权引用影响指数（FWCI），并控制地理、经济、人口、政治因素及内生网络过程。

Result: 结果支持了双向共演化假设。地理距离会调节科研绩效与网络动态之间的互动，研究者更依赖可见的绩效指标来选择地理距离较远的合作者。

Conclusion: 证实了国际合作网络与国家科研绩效之间存在双向因果共演化关系，揭示了基于引文的绩效指标在地理距离较远的合作者选择中充当信号机制的作用。

Abstract: Researchers have long suspected that international research collaboration (IRC) and scientific and technological (S\&T) performance are subject to reciprocal causality, yet the endogenous co-evolution of these twin phenomena has yet to be tested by large-scale empirical analysis. This study tests IRC network effects on national research performance and vice versa simultaneously using a longitudinal co-evolution model on three decades of global network and national performance data. Stochastic actor oriented models (SAOM) are used to analyze data on 166 countries from 1993 to 2022. Yearly IRC networks are constructed from Web of Science's XML database, and performance data are gathered from Elsevier's fractional field-weighted citation index (FWCI). The models also account for geographic, economic, demographic, and political factors, as well as endogenous network processes. The results provide support for reciprocal co-evolution. However, notably, geographic distance appears to moderate the interaction between research performance and network dynamics, suggesting researchers may rely more on visible performance metrics when selecting geographically distant collaborators. This finding points to the role of citation based performance metrics as a signaling mechanism for collaborator selection.

### [185] [Opinion Polarization in LLM-Based Social Networks: Manipulation and Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18795)
*Ali Safarpoor Dehkordi,Mohammad Shirzadi,Ahad N. Zehmakan*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文首次在基于LLM的仿真社交网络框架中系统分析了意见极化放大与缓解问题，发现即使有限预算的对手也能显著增加极化，且现有防御机制无法完全恢复网络基线极化状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数学模型虽能研究意见极化的放大与缓解，但其简化假设（如互动方式、消息内容、意见更新）限制了可捕获的对抗策略及现实适用性。LLM仿真提供了更丰富的替代方案，能够研究经典模型难以表达的操纵策略。本文首次在LLM仿真社交网络框架中系统分析极化放大与缓解问题。

Method: 构建LLM代理仿真社交网络框架，代理被赋予多样化人格，通过自然语言发帖互动并根据内容更新意见。研究两类防御机制：反应性缓解（指定特定用户主动反击操纵）和主动性干预（通过通用机制增加整体抵抗力，不针对特定用户）。

Result: 即使拥有有限操纵预算的对手也能显著增加意见极化。两类防御机制虽能降低攻击影响，但通常无法将网络恢复到基线极化状态。

Conclusion: 现有防御方法均无法完全克服网络对操纵的脆弱性，凸显了此类攻击的潜在风险。

Abstract: How vulnerable are online social networks to adversaries who seek to amplify opinion polarization by manipulating opinions, and how difficult is it to mitigate such manipulation? Existing studies have examined this question using mathematical models of opinion dynamics. While these models offer valuable theoretical insights, they rely on simplified assumptions about interactions, message content, and opinion updates, limiting the adversarial strategies they can capture and the applicability of their findings to real-world settings. Large language model (LLM)-based simulations provide a richer alternative: agents can be assigned diverse personas, communicate through natural language, and respond to persuasive or adversarial content in a context-dependent way. This enables the study of manipulation strategies that are difficult to represent using classical mathematical models. To the best of our knowledge, this study provides the first systematic analysis of polarization amplification and mitigation in an LLM-based simulated social network framework.
  In our framework, LLM agents with diverse personas interact over a social network by exchanging natural language posts and updating their opinions accordingly. We show that even an adversary with a limited manipulation budget can considerably increase polarization. We then study two classes of defense mechanisms: reactive mitigations, which assign specific users to actively counter manipulation, and proactive interventions, which increase resistance through general mechanisms not tied to particular users. Our results show that although these mechanisms reduce the impact of adversarial attacks, they generally do not restore the network to its baseline polarization state. These findings suggest that neither approach fully overcomes the vulnerability of the network, highlighting the potential risk of such attacks.

</details>


### [186] [Digital Speech Acts Retain Control of Copyright with People, Not Platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19263)
*James Golike,Ehud Shapiro*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出"数字言语行为"概念——个人用自己的私钥在自有设备上对内容进行密码签名，论证该行为符合美国版权法保护条件（Burrow-Giles的意志性创造、Feist的最低创造性、设备存储满足固定要求），并认为草根平台（点对点架构）通过设计保护此版权，从而实现数字主权和民主自治。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律先例将计算机代码作为版权表达保护，但这反而促成了中心化数字平台通过版权、合同与技术架构的结合构建私人治理体系——用户为参与平台不得不通过服务条款放弃有效版权控制。作者旨在探索去中心化的替代方案。

Method: 定义"数字言语行为"概念，并运用美国版权法先例（Burrow-Giles、Feist）及版权法固定要求进行法律论证；同时阐述草根平台（无服务器、个人持有数据）的技术架构如何从设计上保护这一版权。

Result: 论证得出：(1) 数字言语行为符合Burrow-Giles的意志性创造要求、满足Feist的最低创造性门槛，且设备持久存储满足固定要求；(2) 草根平台的数字社会契约通过设计保护版权——签名内容不可与签名分离，转发时累积完整溯源链；(3) 数字言语行为中的版权是数字主权和民主自治的前提。

Conclusion: 数字言语行为的版权保护是草根平台实现数字主权和民主自治的法律基础，为去中心化数字治理提供了版权法层面的可行性论证。

Abstract: Legal precedents protect computer code as copyrightable expression. They have enabled centralized digital platforms -- operating from corporate servers that hold all user data -- to construct private governance regimes through the interaction of copyright, contract, and technical architecture: people who create virtually all platform value must surrender effective copyright control through Terms of Service agreements as a condition of participation.
  In contrast, grassroots platforms consist of cryptographically-identified people operating their networked smartphones independently of any server or global resource; each person holds their own data on their own device, with no third party in possession or intermediation. Here, we define the notion of a \textit{digital speech act} -- a deliberate volitional act by a person of cryptographically signing personal content with the person's private key, carried out on the person's own device -- through which the person simultaneously establishes attribution, accountability, and authorship over the signed content. We contend that (\ia) digital speech acts qualify for copyright protection under existing U.S.\ precedent: \textit{Burrow-Giles} locates authorship in volitional creative choices despite mechanical or algorithmic processes, \textit{Feist} supplies the minimal-creativity threshold, and persistent device storage satisfies the Copyright Act's fixation requirement; (\ib) the digital social contract underlying grassroots platforms preserves this copyright by design -- signed content cannot be unbundled from its signature, and the full provenance chain accumulates as content is forwarded -- so that ownership and possession coalesce in the person; and (\ic) copyright in digital speech acts is a prerequisite for digital sovereignty and democratic self-governance.

</details>

It arguably represents what the field of programming has been building towards since the beginning, with every higher level of abstraction that is conceived. ### [188] [Exploring Statistical Change Point Detection Techniques for Performance Anomaly Detection at Mozilla](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18377)
*Mohamed Bilel Besbes,Gregory Mierzwinski,Suhaib Mujahid,Philipp Leitner,Alexander Serebrenik,Dave Hunt,Diego Elias Costa*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文对Mozilla的Perfherder系统（基于T检验）进行了实证研究，评估了25种变化点检测方法和15种集成方法。基于174个由11名工程师标注的真实性能时间序列数据，发现离线/混合方法提高召回率但降低精度，而集成投票策略能有效缓解这一权衡，F1分数提升11%。研究结果已通过实践者调查验证，并报告了集成到Mozilla系统的经验教训。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mozilla的Perfherder系统基于Student's T-test检测性能回归，但实际数据表明其存在12.5%的误报率和约6.8%的漏报率，迫切需要更准确的替代方法。

Method: 构建了由11名Mozilla性能工程师人工标注的174个性能时间序列数据集，系统性评估了25种变化点检测方法和15种集成方法，并通过实践者调查验证结果。

Result: 离线与混合CPD方法虽提高了召回率，但严重降低了精度；集成投票策略则能有效平衡召回率与精度，F1分数较Mozilla现有方法提升11%。

Conclusion: 集成投票方法优于单一CPD方法，更适合实际性能工程中的回归检测场景，且研究已部分集成到Mozilla系统并总结了经验教训。

Abstract: Software performance regressions can have significant business consequences, making automated detection a critical component of modern continuous integration pipelines. At Mozilla, performance anomaly detection is handled by Perfherder, Mozilla's performance engineering management system that relies on a Student's T-test-based approach to flag regressions across hundreds of daily code changes. However, our preliminary analysis of one year of Mozilla performance data reveals that 12.5% of generated alert groups are false positives, while approximately 6.8% of them contain regressions missed by the automated system.
  This paper presents an empirical study evaluating 25 change-point detection (CPD) methods and 15 ensemble approaches as alternatives to Mozilla's current method. We construct a ground-truth dataset of 174 performance time series manually annotated by eleven Mozilla performance engineers, representing one of the first practitioner-annotated CPD benchmarks for performance engineering. Our results show that while offline and hybrid CPD methods improve recall over Mozilla's method, they do so at a high cost to precision. Ensemble voting strategies alleviate this trade-off and offer more consistent performance, resulting in 11% improvement in the F1-score. We validate the experimental results through a practitioner survey and report on lessons learned from integrating the best methods into Mozilla's performance engineering system.

### [189] [Finding Compiler-Platform Interaction Bugs in Deep Learning Pipelines via Cross-Layer Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18421)
*Yuxin Qiu,Jiyuan Wang,Ronak Badhe,Ben Limpanukorn,Miryung Kim,Qian Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出XCheck框架，通过提取全栈约束来自动化测试深度学习编译器（如TVM、ONNX-MLIR），成功发现2,034个编译器-平台交互缺陷，包括内存溢出、整数溢出和静默未预期编译等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DL编译器测试方法主要关注类型约束和输入生成限制，忽略了编译栈与执行平台之间交互导致的缺陷（compiler-platform interaction bugs），亟需能够捕捉这种跨编译pass和硬件平台交互效应的自动化测试框架。

Method: 三阶段方法：(1) 自动提取全栈约束，联合指导模型生成并表征编译行为；(2) 优先筛选对交互敏感的约束，生成能触发深层编译逻辑的模型；(3) 通过自动插入断言实现行为等价划分，捕获覆盖率或通过/失败信号无法监测的编译症状。

Result: 在三个广泛使用的DL编译器上评估XCheck，发现2,034个缺陷暴露案例，涵盖内存溢出、整数溢出以及静默未预期编译等由编译器-平台交互引起的错误。

Conclusion: 提出了一种超越传统类型约束的、可扩展的自动化DL编译器测试框架，通过全栈约束有效发现编译器与硬件平台交互带来的深层缺陷。

Abstract: The growing deployment of artificial intelligence (AI) necessitates robust deep learning (DL) compilers, such as TVM and ONNX-MLIR. These compilers take as input high-level AI models, lower them through multi-layer transformations, and specialize them to diverse hardware. Testing such compilers is uniquely challenging as correctness depends on implicit constraints embedded throughout the compilation stack. Existing testing approaches largely take type constraints to restrict input model generation and therefore emphasize type validation and monitor compilation crashes or coverage gains. This focus overlooks compiler-platform interaction bugs that arise from interleaved effects across compilation and execution environments.
  In this work, we propose a scalable, automated DL compiler testing framework for, in tandem, (1) finding compiler-platform interaction bugs and (2) enabling behavior equivalence partitioning. Our key insight is that these bugs are caused by violated assumptions arising from interactions across compilation passes and hardware platforms. Therefore, we move beyond constraining input generation and derive full-stack constraints. Our approach is three-fold. First, we design an automated approach to extract full-stack constraints that jointly guide model generation and characterize compilation behaviors. Second, we prioritize constraints that expose interaction-sensitive behaviors, so our generated models are capable of exercising deep compilation logic. Third, we enable behavior equivalence partitioning by automatically inserting assertions to monitor distinct compilation symptoms that coverage or pass/fail signals miss.
  We evaluated our tool, XCheck, on three widely-used DL compilers and found 2,034 bug-revealing cases, including memory overflows, integer overflows, and silent unexpected compilations that were rooted in compiler-platform interactions.

</details>


### [190] [A Critical Discourse Analysis of Gender Representation in Software Engineering Education Videos on YouTube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18423)
*Isabella Graßl,Alexander Serebrenik,Giuseppe Destefanis*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究对YouTube上200个英德软件工程教程进行批判性话语分析，发现男性角色和男性化语言占主导，女性被边缘化或被赋予被动角色，形成“能动性鸿沟”，这可能构成女性进入软件工程领域的象征性障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件工程领域长期存在性别差距，而教育资源（包括在线学习内容）可能影响学生对“谁适合这个领域”的认知。然而，关于在线学习空间中与性别相关的“隐性课程”知之甚少，因此有必要揭示YouTube教程中性别表征的现状。

Method: 采用批判性话语分析方法，对YouTube上200个英文和德文软件工程教程进行手工标注和分析，聚焦语境领域（contextual domains）和语言身份标记（linguistic identity markers），考察性别表征模式。

Result: 男性角色和男性化语言默认占主导地位；存在明显的“能动性鸿沟”（agency gap），技术和决策角色几乎全由男性承担，女性要么缺席，要么被赋予被动、低能动性的角色。

Conclusion: YouTube上的软件工程教育可能再生产了性别化的规范，语言和表征上的“守门”行为构成了女性进入软件工程领域的象征性障碍，暗示了隐性课程在维持性别不平等中的作用。

Abstract: Educational resources may frame students' perceptions of who belongs in software engineering, which is relevant given the field's ongoing gender gap. However, we know little about the hidden curriculum regarding gender in online learning spaces. This study presents a critical discourse analysis of 200 manually analysed English and German software engineering tutorials on YouTube, examining gender representation through contextual domains and linguistic identity markers. Our results show that male characters and masculine linguistic defaults dominate the tutorials. We identified an agency gap, in which technical and decision-making roles are almost exclusively assigned to male actors, while female actors are either absent or tend to passive, low-agency roles. The findings indicate that software engineering education on YouTube may reproduce gendered norms, in which linguistic and representational gatekeeping may serve as a symbolic barrier to software engineering.

</details>


### [191] [From Specification to Execution: AI Assisted Scientific Workflow Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18425)
*Komal Thareja,Hamza Safri,Rajiv Mayani,Anirban Mandal,Ewa Deelman*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合规范驱动工作流生成、自动调试和分布式执行的AI辅助科学工作流管理方法，通过结构化规范阶段分离意图、设计与实现，并集成Pegasus与MCP层，在医学影像联邦学习工作流上验证了其可行性，减少了调试工作量，使非专家用户也能构建专家级工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学工作流管理系统虽然支持可扩展和可复现的执行，但工作流的设计、实现和调试仍然高度依赖人工和专业经验。现有基于LLM的方法虽能生成工作流，但多依赖直接代码合成，缺乏透明性、可复现性和与工作流系统的良好集成。

Method: 提出了一种AI辅助方法，包括三个阶段：(1) 结构化规范阶段，分离工作流意图、设计和实现，在代码生成前进行验证；(2) 基于LLM的调试代理，跨多层系统诊断和解决故障；(3) 将Pegasus WMS与模型上下文协议（MCP）层集成，提供统一的工作流提交、监控和控制接口。

Result: 在医学影像联邦学习工作流上评估，系统生成并执行了包含数千个任务的大规模工作流，减少了调试工作量，并使非专家用户能够构建出具有专家级设计模式的工作流。

Conclusion: 端到端的AI辅助工作流生成与执行是可行的，未来可朝着AI驱动的科学工作流生命周期管理平台方向发展。

Abstract: Scientific workflow management systems (WMS) support scalable and reproducible execution of complex pipelines, but workflow design, implementation, and debugging remain largely manual and require significant expertise. Recent approaches using large language models (LLMs) show promise for workflow generation from natural language, but often rely on direct code synthesis, which limits transparency, reproducibility, and integration with workflow systems. We present an AI-assisted approach to scientific workflow management that combines specification-driven workflow generation, automated debugging, and distributed execution. The method introduces a structured specification phase that separates workflow intent, design, and implementation, allowing validation prior to code generation. We also develop an LLM-based debugging agent that diagnoses and resolves failures across multiple system layers. To support distributed execution and user interaction, we integrate Pegasus, a widely used WMS, with a Model Context Protocol (MCP) layer, providing a unified interface for workflow submission, monitoring, and control. We evaluate the approach using a federated learning workflow for medical imaging, chosen for its parallel, iterative, and dependency-intensive structure. The system generated and executed large-scale workflows with thousands of jobs, reduced debugging effort, and allowed non-expert users to construct workflows with expert-level design patterns. These results indicate that end-to-end AI-assisted workflow generation and execution is feasible, and point toward AI-driven platforms for managing the scientific workflow lifecycle.

*Qiao Zhao,JianYing Qu,Jun Zhang,Yehua Yang,Hanwen Du,Zhongkai Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出SWE-Future方法，利用仓库历史证据预测未来开发任务，合成面向未来的编程智能体数据集，避免直接回放历史issue/PR导致的数据污染问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编程智能体基准测试常回放公开GitHub issue/PR，与模型预训练数据存在重叠风险；完全合成任务又可能偏离真实仓库需求。

Method: 在时间点T₀基于T₀之前的仓库证据预测未来任务（功能实现、bug修复、重构三类）；用T₀之后实际发生的PR验证预测相关性；将验证有效的预测作为条件信号合成200个任务的编程智能体数据集。

Result: 在80个仓库的回顾性验证中，预测器在主要语义匹配指标上达到58.1%的未来工作相关性；最终合成了61个仓库上的200个任务数据集。

Abstract: Realistic coding-agent benchmarks often replay public GitHub issues and pull requests, making them vulnerable to overlap with model pretraining, fine-tuning, synthetic-data generation, or benchmark-driven model selection. Fully synthetic tasks avoid direct historical replay, but can drift away from real repository needs. We propose SWE-Future, a forecast-conditioned data synthesis method for future-oriented coding tasks. Given a forecast snapshot at time $T_0$, the method uses only pre-$T_0$ repository evidence to forecast future feature implementation/enhancement, bugfix, and refactor task families. We first validate this forecasting step retrospectively: after forecasts are fixed, later pull requests are used only to measure whether the predicted task families match future repository work. In an 80-repository study, the forecaster achieves 58.1\% future-work relevance under the main semantic matching metric. We then use validated forecast families as conditioning signals to synthesize a 200-task coding-agent dataset across 61 repositories from a task-generation snapshot, rather than replaying the later pull requests used for validation. SWE-Future shows that repository-evolution forecasts can guide realistic, future-oriented coding-task synthesis while reducing direct dependence on historical pull-request replay.

### [194] [Toward Semantically-Seeded, Graph-Propagated Impact Analysis Across Software Artifacts: A Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18855)
*Momil Seedat*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需训练、可解释的融合分析方法，同时利用语义相似性（文本嵌入）和结构依赖（静态分析构建的异构图传播）来检测软件变更的影响，弥补单一方法的盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有变更影响分析工具分别依赖语义相似性或结构依赖，各自存在盲点：语义方法遗漏无词汇重叠的受影响工件，结构方法遗漏无直接依赖但语义相关的工件，且大多只分析代码而非需求-配置-服务-测试全链路。

Method: 将系统建模为异构工件图（边由静态分析恢复），通过余弦相似度计算变工件语义先验，利用行归一化传播矩阵进行多跳衰减传播，再用单可调权重λ融合语义层和传播层结果。

Result: 在支付子系统的5个标注变更场景上的概念验证表明：零文本重叠的工件可通过传播恢复，传播无法触及的辅助函数可通过语义层恢复，融合是唯一能覆盖两类盲点的配置，λ可作为精确率/召回率的显式控制旋钮。

Conclusion: 该融合方法不仅适用于代码分析，还可扩展到操作工件（镜像、指标、仪表盘、数据模式等），弥补传统仅代码分析无法覆盖的盲区。

Abstract: When a single software artifact changes - a requirement, a configuration value, or a function - engineers must determine what else is impacted. Existing change-impact-analysis (CIA) tooling tends to rely on one of two signals in isolation: semantic similarity recovered from text (information-retrieval traceability, code search, embeddings), or structural dependency following (call graphs, IDE "find usages", test-impact selection). Each has a characteristic blind spot. A semantically driven tool misses an impacted artifact whose text shares no vocabulary with the change; a structurally driven tool misses artifacts related in meaning but not joined by an edge, and most operate only over code rather than the Requirement-Config-Service-Test chain. We argue for a training-free and interpretable analyzer that fuses both signals over the same embeddings. We model the system as a heterogeneous artifact graph with typed edges recovered by static analysis, compute a semantic prior by cosine similarity to the changed artifact, propagate impact multi-hop with decay over a row-normalized propagation matrix, and blend the two with a single tunable weight lambda. A small but complete proof-of-concept on a payment subsystem (5 labelled change scenarios) shows the mechanism we care about: artifacts with zero textual overlap with the change are still recovered through propagation, and helper functions that propagation alone cannot reach are recovered through the semantic layer. The fusion is the only configuration that covers both blind spots, and lambda acts as an explicit precision/recall control. Drawing on four publicly documented production failures, we argue that the same formulation extends to operational artifacts (images, metrics, dashboards, data schemas) that code-only analysis cannot reach.

This paper presents CAPRA (Configurable Architecture Proficiency Report Assessment), a multi-agent LLM system that analyzes software architecture deliverables to generate personalized, template-compliant LaTeX feedback. As a core design choice, CAPRA coordinates multiple specialized agents and employs a Python-based microservice for multi-modal document extraction, utilizing PyMuPDF and vision-enabled LLMs (specifically gpt-4o) to parse text and UML diagrams. System performance is assessed using a structured eight-criterion binary evaluation taxonomy covering: (i) extraction completeness, (ii) feature validation, (iii) issue grounding and severity detection, (iv) recommendation specificity and traceability, and (v) template and tone compliance. A preliminary empirical evaluation on 10 student reports shows that CAPRA satisfied 88.8% of the evaluated criteria under a strict two-rater aggregation rule, achieved moderate inter-rater agreement with human evaluators (kappa = 0.582), and processed each report in slightly over 4 minutes. ### [196] [Where Did the Variability Go? From Vibe Coding to Product Lines by Regeneration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19042)
*Xhevahire Tërnava*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文发现AI编程（vibe coding）生成的代码在编译和运行时几乎没有可变性，所有可变性决策都被固化在LLM生成代码的那一刻。作者提出"通过再生实现可变性"（VbR），让LLM作为推导引擎，根据声明式规范为每个变体生成无死代码的二进制程序，并透明路由用户请求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统软件工程通过代码精心构建可变性，但AI驱动编程（LLM直接从自然语言生成完整程序）是否还保留这种可变性？这一未知问题促使作者进行探索性分析。

Method: 对10个通过vibe coding生成的C/C++项目进行探索性分析，发现近零的构件内可变性。随后提出Variability by Regeneration (VbR)方法：LLM作为推导引擎，从声明式规范为每个变体生成专用二进制程序，配合变体分发器透明路由用户请求。

Result: 1) vibe coding产生的代码在编译和运行时几乎没有可变性；2) 所有可变性决策在LLM生成源代码的"生成时"就已被解决；3) VbR被形式化，与传统SPL推导形成对比；4) 在wc产品家族上完整演示了VbR流水线。

Conclusion: 在AI生成软件的SPL工程中，可变性应存在于规范（specification）中，而非代码中。LLM在生成时一次性解决所有变体决策，避免了传统代码中死代码和条件编译的复杂性。

Abstract: In vibe coding, an emerging AI-driven paradigm, an LLM generates an entire program from a natural language prompt, but what happens to the variability that traditional software engineering carefully builds into code? To answer this question, we conducted an exploratory analysis on 10 vibe coded C/C++ projects, which suggests that there is near-zero in-artifact variability, i.e., at compile and runtime. All variability decisions are resolved at a single new binding time, generation time, the moment the LLM produces the source code. Rather than treating this as a defect to fix, we propose Variability by Regeneration (VbR), to our knowledge the first product-line approach in which the LLM acts as the derivation engine, generating a purpose-built, free of dead code binary for each variant from a declarative specification, while a variant dispatcher transparently routes user requests to the matching binary. We formalise VbR, contrast it with classical SPL derivation, and demonstrate its full pipeline on a wc product family. For SPL engineering, variability in AI-generated software belongs in the specification, not in the code.

### [197] [Written by AI, Managed by AI: Semantic Space Control and Index Sickness Elimination Across 391 Consecutive Sessions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19121)
*Hui Zhang,Shuren Song*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过一个为期约一月、391次协作会话的真实软件项目（Bang-v3），揭示了在长周期LLM协作中，增加符号约束（如标识系统、防御规则、扩展上下文）反而会导致模型放弃真实语义理解、陷入符号层自指推理的"索引病"（Index Sickness）现象。作者提出"庞氏原理（语义活力法则）"：带明确目的的自然语言比符号表达信息质量更高，并设计了"基线日志物理分离"机制，将AI指令量减少了约75%，后续约150次会话中未再复发该病。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战长周期LLM协作中"越正式约束越可靠"的主流工程直觉，记录并分析该策略在实际项目中出现的反直觉失败过程。

Method: 采用行动研究方法，在Bang-v3真实软件项目中进行约一个月、391次协作会话的工程记录与失败过程分析，随后设计并验证"基线日志物理分离"机制。

Result: 符号系统超过复杂度阈值后，LLM变得不准确，陷入符号层自指推理；提出的"基线日志物理分离"机制将AI指令量减少约75%，后续150次会话无复发。

Conclusion: 过度符号约束适得其反，应回归自然语言的高质量语义表达；"基线日志物理分离"是有效的物理工程机制。

Abstract: The prevailing engineering intuition for addressing conceptual drift in long-horizon LLM collaboration is to trade more formal constraints for more reliable outputs -- designing symbolic identifier systems, accumulating defensive rules in System Prompts, expanding context windows. Our engineering record shows that in long-horizon settings, this direction may produce effects contrary to design intent. Using action research methods in a real software project (Bang-v3) spanning approximately one month and 391 collaborative sessions, we document and analyze the failure process of these strategies. When the symbolic system exceeds a complexity threshold, LLMs do not become more accurate -- instead, they abandon genuine understanding of business semantics, retreat to self-referential reasoning within the symbolic layer, and generate outputs that appear internally consistent but are physically disconnected from reality. We name this failure pattern "Index Sickness," and its canonical manifestation "Phantom Legislation." We name the underlying principle the "Pang Principle (Semantic Vitality Law)": natural language carrying explicit purpose conveys far greater information quality than symbolic expression. From this, we design and validate its physical engineering mechanism: "Baseline-Log Physical Separation." In the same project, this mechanism reduced AI Instructions volume by ~75%, and across the subsequent ~150 sessions, no recurrence of Index Sickness was observed. A bilingual companion version (Chinese) is included as supplementary material.

We provide insights and recommendations for researchers and practitioners on how to design, research, and employ programming assistants to better account for diverse developer needs.

</details>


### [200] [Runtime Compliance Verification for AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19242)
*Nafiseh Kahani,Masoud Barati,Diana Addae*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出C-Trace框架，通过运行时监控工具调用和模型输出，将GDPR合规要求（同意、目的限制、数据最小化、删除权）形式化为策略谓词，在Agent执行过程中实时拦截违规行为。实验显示在完美提取下攻击成功率为0%，在10%噪声下仍低于12%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI Agent安全测试主要依赖离线红队测试或静态提示审查，无法在运行时保证Agent行为符合GDPR等法规要求，迫切需要运行时合规验证机制。

Method: C-Trace框架包含三个组件：(i) 将GDPR部分要求形式化为策略谓词；(ii) 运行时监视器拦截每次工具调用和模型输出，拒绝不合规行为；(iii) 使用DSPy生成提示和红队语料中的逐字提示进行攻击测试。

Result: 在四个GDPR案例研究中，完美提取下ASR为0%；10%提取器噪声下ASR≤12%（低于基线），假阳性率≤16%。

Conclusion: C-Trace能有效在运行时保障AI Agent的GDPR合规性，即使在存在提取噪声的情况下仍能保持较低的违规率和误报率。

Abstract: AI agents now handle personal data through tool use, function calls, and multi turn dialogue, which can create obligations under the General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR). Current testing practices mainly rely on offline red teaming or static prompt review, but they do not guarantee at runtime that agent behavior follows regulatory rules. We propose C-Trace (Compliance Trace based Runtime Agent Conformance Enforcement), a verification framework that: (i) expresses a subset of GDPR requirements, including consent, purpose limitation, data minimization, and the right to erasure, as formal policy predicates over agent execution traces; (ii) uses a runtime monitor that intercepts every tool invocation and model output and rejects non-compliant actions; and (iii) tests the agent with attack dialogues, including DSPy generated prompts and verbatim prompts from red teaming corpora, that try to induce violations. We evaluate the framework on four case studies reframed to GDPR. Under 10 percent per-category extractor noise, including drop-out and over-typing, the monitor keeps the attack success rate at less than or equal to 12 percent, below the baselines we compare against, and false positives at less than or equal to 16 percent, and reaches 0 percent ASR under perfect extraction.

</details>
